Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\n13: \n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure). E.g. version 3\n15: of the tracing API package is named `envoy.service.trace.v3` and its constituent protos are located\n16: in `api/envoy/service/trace/v3`. The template parameters RQ and RS represent the request and response proto types, supporting both v2 (DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse) and v3 (DiscoveryRequest v3/DiscoveryResponse v3) types.\\n   - `sotw_subscription_state.h` and `sotw_subscription_state.cc`: Manages subscription state for SotW protocol with v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `delta_subscription_state.h` and `delta_subscription_state.cc`: Manages subscription state for Delta protocol with v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `subscription_state.h`: Base interface for subscription state management.\\n\\n2. **Legacy GrpcMux Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/):**\\n   - `grpc_mux_impl.h` and `grpc_mux_impl.cc`: Legacy SotW-only GrpcMux implementation using v3 discovery types (envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response).\\n   - `new_grpc_mux_impl.h` and `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc`: New Delta-only GrpcMux implementation using v3 discovery types (envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response).\\n\\n3. **Subscription Factory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/):**\\n   - `grpc_subscription_factory.h` and `grpc_subscription_factory.cc`: Creates subscriptions for SotW GRPC, Delta GRPC, and ADS. The factory handles API version configuration through the `transport_api_version` field in `ApiConfigSource`.\\n\\n4. **Failover Support:**\\n   - `grpc_mux_failover.h`: Implements failover logic between primary and secondary xDS sources with v2/v3 proto type support through template parameters.\\n\\n5. **Resource Decoding and Management:**\\n   - `source/common/config/xds_manager_impl.h` and `xds_manager_impl.cc`: Manages multiple xDS subscriptions with v2/v3 version awareness.\\n   - `source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h` and `subscription_factory_impl.cc`: Creates subscriptions based on ConfigSource configuration.\\n\\n6. **Proto Link Hacks:**\\n   - `source/common/config/protobuf_link_hacks.h`: Forces linking of v3 proto definitions.\\n   - `test/config/v2_link_hacks.h`: Forces linking of v2 proto definitions for testing.\\n\\n**Key Field Renames and Migration Patterns:**\\n\\nThe v2-to-v3 migration is defined in the proto files with `(udpa.annotations.field_migrate)` annotations:\\n- `api/envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto`: Defines v2 DiscoveryRequest and DeltaDiscoveryRequest messages that are annotated to migrate to v3.\\n- `api/envoy/api/v2/core/config_source.proto`: Defines ApiVersion enum with V2 (deprecated) and V3 values, controlling transport API version selection.\\n\\n**ADS gRPC Server and Dual-Version Handling:**\\n\\nThe ADS implementation supports both v2 and v3 through:\\n1. **Runtime Feature Flags**: The unified mux uses `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux` to select between legacy (GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl) and unified implementations (Config::XdsMux::GrpcMuxSotw, Config::XdsMux::GrpcMuxDelta).\\n2. **Template-Based Protocol Handling**: The xds_mux `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` template allows single codebase to handle both SotW and Delta with v2 or v3 proto types.\\n3. **API Version Configuration**: The `transport_api_version` field in `ApiConfigSource` controls which protocol version is used on the wire, while `resource_api_version` controls the resource message versions.\\n\\n**Subscription Lifecycle:**\\n\\nWhen a subscription is created (in `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create`), the factory determines the appropriate Mux implementation based on:\\n1. The API type (GRPC for SotW, DELTA_GRPC for Delta)\\n2. Whether the unified mux feature is enabled\\n3.
